• Findings

  - SumRule-v8.tex:722: Protocol A now says you can use \sum r_\alpha \le 2 via Eq. (Khf-trace) as a “general FS” fallback. But SumRule-v8.tex:669 defines Eq.
  (Khf-trace) for principal-axis ratios in the strong-locking, diagonal-coaxial hyperfine setting, not for arbitrary fixed-axis r_\alpha. The protocol table at
  SumRule-v8.tex:703 still lists Protocol A’s assumption as “3D isotropic FS.” As written, that fallback is not valid.
  - SumRule-v8.tex:526 and SumRule-v8.tex:801 now say the site bound / multiband trace inequality remain valid “regardless” of inter-band or orbitally mixed
  pairing, but SumRule-v8.tex:213 still says trace-bound violation can signal multi-orbital physics. Those scope statements conflict. The manuscript needs one
  consistent position here.
  - SumRule-v8.tex:40 and SumRule-v8.tex:821 again state the K$_2$Cr$_3$As$_3$ data select a rigid common \mathbf d \parallel \hat c / OSP interpretation, while
  SumRule-v8.tex:860 correctly weakens that to a baseline inference within the orbital-diagonal model. Those two conclusion levels should not coexist.

  SumRule-v8.tex does compile, and the reused Wolfram audit check_sumrule_v6.wl still returns clean True checks on the already-audited identities. So the issues
  I found are logical/scope inconsistencies, not a fresh algebra failure in the formulas covered by that script.

  If you want, I can patch these into v9.

› What does the RMS mean? In the appendix


• I’m checking the appendix language in v14 so I can answer against the exact sentence rather than guessing what you intended there.

─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• In the appendix, “RMS” means root-mean-square deviation of the extracted data points from the theoretical curve. See SumRule-v14.tex:913.

  # Here it means
  [
  \mathrm{RMS}

  # \sqrt{\frac{1}{N}\sum_{i=1}^N \left(\Delta_i\right)^2},
  \qquad
  \Delta_i

  ## \left[\frac{\chi(0)}{\chi_N}\right]^{\rm digitized}_i

  \left[\frac{\chi(0)}{\chi_N}\right]^{\rm theory}_i.
  ]

  So:

  - max deviation = 1.5×10^{-3} is the worst mismatch among the extracted points.
  - RMS = 7.7×10^{-4} is the typical mismatch size overall.

  In this appendix, it is the RMS over the extracted (T=0) intercepts used for the Fig. 3 cross-check.

  If you want, I can change the text to say “root-mean-square deviation” explicitly so the appendix is clearer.

      1 +(* Wolfram audit for the algebra used in SumRule-v17.tex. *)
      2 +
      3 +ClearAll["Global`*"];
      4 +
      5 +reportLines = {};
      6 +status = <||>;
      7 +passCount = 0;
      8 +failCount = 0;
      9 +reviewCount = 0;
     10 +
     11 +say[str_] := (
     12 +  AppendTo[reportLines, str];
     13 +  Print[str];
     14 +);
     15 +
     16 +section[name_] := say["\n=== " <> name <> " ==="];
     17 +
     18 +markPass[label_, note_] := (
     19 +  status[label] = <|"status" -> "PASS", "note" -> note|>;
     20 +  passCount++;
     21 +  say["[PASS]   " <> label <> "  " <> note];
     22 +);
     23 +
     24 +markFail[label_, note_] := (
     25 +  status[label] = <|"status" -> "FAIL", "note" -> note|>;
     26 +  failCount++;
     27 +  say["[FAIL]   " <> label <> "  " <> note];
     28 +);
     29 +
     30 +markReview[label_, note_] := (
     31 +  status[label] = <|"status" -> "REVIEW", "note" -> note|>;
     32 +  reviewCount++;
     33 +  say["[REVIEW] " <> label <> "  " <> note];
     34 +);
     35 +
     36 +markMany[labels_, fun_, note_] := Scan[fun[#, note] &, labels];
     37 +
     38 +checkExact[label_, note_, expr_, asm_: True] := Module[{res},
     39 +  res = Quiet@FullSimplify[expr, asm];
     40 +  If[TrueQ[res],
     41 +    markPass[label, note],
     42 +    markFail[label, note <> " -> " <> ToString[res, InputForm]]
     43 +  ]
     44 +];
     45 +
     46 +maxAbs[m_] := Max[Abs[Flatten[N[m, 30]]]];
     47 +
     48 +checkNumericScalar[label_, note_, lhs_, rhs_, tol_: 10.^-10] := Module[{diff},
     49 +  diff = N[Abs[lhs - rhs], 30];
     50 +  If[NumericQ[diff] && diff <= tol,
     51 +    markPass[label, note <> ", abs diff = " <> ToString[NumberForm[diff, {10, 3}], InputForm]],
     52 +    markFail[label, note <> ", abs diff = " <> ToString[NumberForm[diff, {10, 3}], InputForm]]
     53 +  ]
     54 +];
     55 +
     56 +checkNumericMatrix[label_, note_, lhs_, rhs_, tol_: 10.^-10] := Module[{diff},
     57 +  diff = maxAbs[lhs - rhs];
     58 +  If[NumericQ[diff] && diff <= tol,
     59 +    markPass[label, note <> ", max abs diff = " <> ToString[NumberForm[diff, {10, 3}], InputForm]],
     60 +    markFail[label, note <> ", max abs diff = " <> ToString[NumberForm[diff, {10, 3}], InputForm]]
     61 +  ]
     62 +];
     63 +
     64 +unitarySample[n_Integer] := Module[{m, q, r, phase},
     65 +  m = RandomReal[{-1, 1}, {n, n}] + I RandomReal[{-1, 1}, {n, n}];
     66 +  {q, r} = QRDecomposition[m];
     67 +  phase = Diagonal[r];
     68 +  phase = Replace[phase/Abs[phase], Indeterminate -> 1, {1}];
     69 +  q . DiagonalMatrix[Conjugate[phase]]
     70 +];
     71 +
     72 +SeedRandom[20260512];

     99 +section["Observable Embedding and Plancherel Identity"];
    100 +
    101 +Omat = {{oa, oc + I od}, {oc - I od, ob}};
    102 +OBdG = (1/2) ArrayFlatten[{{Omat, ConstantArray[0, {2, 2}]}, {ConstantArray[0, {2, 2}], -Transpose[Omat]}}];
    103 +
    104 +checkExact[
    105 +  "eq:Oembedding",
    106 +  "BdG embedding is Hermitian",
    107 +  ConjugateTranspose[OBdG] == OBdG,
    108 +  Element[{oa, ob, oc, od}, Reals]
    109 +];
    110 +
    111 +checkExact[
    112 +  "eq:BdGtrace",
    113 +  "BdG trace vanishes",
    114 +  Tr[OBdG] == 0,
    115 +  Element[{oa, ob, oc, od}, Reals]
    116 +];
    117 +
    118 +checkExact[
    119 +  "eq:BdGtrace:norm",
    120 +  "BdG Frobenius norm is half the single-particle norm",
    121 +  Tr[OBdG . OBdG] == (1/2) Tr[Omat . Omat],
    122 +  Element[{oa, ob, oc, od}, Reals]
    123 +];
    124 +
    125 +Module[{u, v, um, vm, Otest, OBtest, Utest, expr, mph, mpp},
    126 +  Otest = {{2.0, 1.0 - 0.7 I}, {1.0 + 0.7 I, -0.4}};
    127 +  u = {{0.7 + 0.1 I, -0.2 + 0.3 I}, {0.5 - 0.4 I, -0.6 + 0.2 I}};
    128 +  v = {{-0.3 + 0.8 I, 0.2 - 0.5 I}, {0.1 + 0.6 I, 0.4 + 0.2 I}};
    129 +  um = {{0.2 - 0.7 I, 0.4 + 0.1 I}, {-0.5 + 0.3 I, 0.6 + 0.4 I}};
    130 +  vm = {{0.3 + 0.2 I, -0.8 + 0.1 I}, {0.5 - 0.6 I, -0.1 + 0.4 I}};
    131 +  OBtest = (1/2) ArrayFlatten[{{Otest, ConstantArray[0, {2, 2}]}, {ConstantArray[0, {2, 2}], -Transpose[Otest]}}];
    132 +  Utest = ArrayFlatten[{{u, v}, {Conjugate[vm], Conjugate[um]}}];
    133 +  expr = ConjugateTranspose[Utest].OBtest.Utest;
    134 +  mph = ConjugateTranspose[u].Otest.u - Transpose[ConjugateTranspose[vm].Otest.vm];
    135 +  mpp = ConjugateTranspose[u].Otest.v - Transpose[ConjugateTranspose[um].Otest.vm];
    136 +  checkNumericMatrix["eq:block", "upper-left block matches the stated particle-hole block", expr[[1 ;; 2, 1 ;; 2]], mph/2];
    137 +  checkNumericMatrix["eq:Mph-O", "particle-hole matrix-element formula matches direct multiplication", expr[[1 ;; 2, 1 ;; 2]], mph/2];
    138 +  checkNumericMatrix["eq:Mpp-O", "particle-particle matrix-element formula matches direct multiplication", expr[[1 ;; 2, 3 ;; 4]], mpp/2];
    139 +];
    140 +

    208 +section["Helicity-Basis Spin Matrix Elements and Strong Locking"];
    209 +
    210 +spinPlus[th_, ph_] := {Cos[th/2], Exp[I ph] Sin[th/2]};
    211 +spinMinus[th_, ph_] := {-Exp[-I ph] Sin[th/2], Cos[th/2]};
    212 +Uhelicity[th_, ph_] := Transpose[{spinPlus[th, ph], spinMinus[th, ph]}];
    213 +nvec[th_, ph_] := {
    214 +  Sin[th] Cos[ph],
    215 +  Sin[th] Sin[ph],
    216 +  Cos[th]
    217 +};
    218 +
    219 +Do[
    220 +  Module[{rot, n, diagNorm, offNorm},
    221 +    rot = FullSimplify[ConjugateTranspose[Uhelicity[th, ph]].paulis[[mu]].Uhelicity[th, ph], Element[{th, ph}, Reals]];
    222 +    n = nvec[th, ph];
    223 +    diagNorm = FullSimplify[Sum[Abs[rot[[s, s]]]^2, {s, 1, 2}], Element[{th, ph}, Reals]];
    224 +    offNorm = FullSimplify[Sum[Abs[rot[[s1, s2]]]^2, {s1, 1, 2}, {s2, 1, 2}] - diagNorm, Element[{th, ph}, Reals]];
    225 +    checkExact[
    226 +      "eq:me-intra:mu" <> ToString[mu],
    227 +      "diagonal helicity weight matches 2 (n . e_mu)^2",
    228 +      diagNorm == 2 n[[mu]]^2,
    229 +      Element[{th, ph}, Reals]
    230 +    ];
    231 +    checkExact[
    232 +      "eq:me-inter:mu" <> ToString[mu],
    233 +      "off-diagonal helicity weight matches 2 [1 - (n . e_mu)^2]",
    234 +      ComplexExpand[TrigReduce[offNorm - 2 (1 - n[[mu]]^2)], {th, ph}] == 0,
    235 +      Element[{th, ph}, Reals]
    236 +    ];
    237 +    checkExact[
    238 +      "eq:paritymix-sigma-helicity:mu" <> ToString[mu],
    239 +      "helicity-basis spin operator has tau_3 coefficient n_mu",
    240 +      rot[[1, 1]] == n[[mu]] && rot[[2, 2]] == -n[[mu]],
    241 +      Element[{th, ph}, Reals]
    242 +    ];
    243 +  ],
    244 +  {mu, 1, 3}
    245 +];
    246 +
    247 +checkExact[
    248 +  "eq:phpartsTc",
    249 +  "normal-state intra- and inter-helicity weights add to chi_N",
    250 +  pi + (1 - pi) == 1,
    251 +  Element[pi, Reals]
    252 +];
    253 +
    254 +checkExact[
    255 +  "eq:strongSOCid",
    256 +  "strong-locking tensor has trace 2 for a unit locking vector",

    258 +  Element[{nx, ny, nz}, Reals] && nx^2 + ny^2 + nz^2 == 1
    259 +];

    283 +

    317 +section["Intermediate-SOC Closed Form"];
    318 +
    319 +f[u_, lam_] := Sqrt[(u + lam)^2 + 1];
    320 +g[u_, lam_] := Sqrt[(u - lam)^2 + 1];
    321 +integrand[u_, lam_] :=
    322 +  (f[u, lam] g[u, lam] - (u + lam) (u - lam) - 1)/
    323 +  (f[u, lam] g[u, lam] (f[u, lam] + g[u, lam]));
    324 +Fs[lam_] := 1 - ArcSinh[lam]/(lam Sqrt[1 + lam^2]);
    325 +
    326 +Do[
    327 +  Module[{lhs, rhs},
    328 +    lhs = NIntegrate[
    329 +      integrand[u, lam0],
    330 +      {u, -Infinity, Infinity},
    331 +      WorkingPrecision -> 50,
    332 +      AccuracyGoal -> 20,
    333 +      PrecisionGoal -> 20
    334 +    ];
    335 +    rhs = N[2 Fs[lam0], 50];
    336 +    checkNumericScalar[
    337 +      "eq:Jdef:eq:Fs:lam=" <> ToString[lam0, InputForm],
    338 +      "direct integral matches the closed form for 1/2 J~ = F_s",
    339 +      lhs,
    340 +      rhs,
    341 +      10.^-20
    342 +    ];
    343 +  ],
    344 +  {lam0, {0.3, 1, 2, 5}}
    345 +];
    346 +
    347 +u2[a_, lam_] := a^2 (a^2 - lam^2 - 1)/(a^2 - lam^2);
    348 +fg[a_, lam_] := ((a^2 - lam^2)^2 + lam^2)/(a^2 - lam^2);
    349 +
    350 +checkExact[
    351 +  "eq:Fs:key-identity",
    352 +  "ellipse parametrization identity used in the closed-form derivation",
    353 +  fg[a, lam] - u2[a, lam] + lam^2 - 1 == 2 lam^2/(a^2 - lam^2),
    354 +  Element[{a, lam}, Reals] && lam > 0 && a > Sqrt[1 + lam^2]
    355 +];
    356 +
    357 +checkExact["eq:Fs:limit0", "F_s(0) = 0", Limit[Fs[lam], lam -> 0] == 0];
    358 +checkExact["eq:Fs:limitInf", "F_s(infinity) = 1", Limit[Fs[lam], lam -> Infinity] == 1];
    359 +
    360 +checkExact[
    361 +  "eq:Fs:series",
    362 +  "small-lambda series matches the stated expansion",
    363 +  Normal@Series[Fs[lam], {lam, 0, 6}] == (2 lam^2)/3 - (8 lam^4)/15 + (16 lam^6)/35
    364 +];
    365 +
    366 +nhat = {nx, ny, nz};
    367 +ehat = {ex, ey, ez};
    368 +chiTensor = Fsc (IdentityMatrix[3] - Outer[Times, nhat, nhat]);
    369 +directionalK = FullSimplify[ehat . chiTensor . ehat, Element[{ex, ey, ez, nx, ny, nz, Fsc}, Reals] && ex^2 + ey^2 + ez^2 == 1];
    370 +
    371 +checkExact[
    372 +  "eq:chi-explicit",
    373 +  "directional response from the dressed projector tensor",
    374 +  directionalK == Fsc (1 - (ehat . nhat)^2),
    375 +  Element[{ex, ey, ez, nx, ny, nz, Fsc}, Reals] && ex^2 + ey^2 + ez^2 == 1
    376 +];
    377 +
    378 +checkExact[
    379 +  "eq:chi-explicit:trace",
    380 +  "intermediate-SOC trace contracts by 2 <F_s>",
    381 +  Tr[chiTensor] == 2 Fsc,
    382 +  Element[{nx, ny, nz, Fsc}, Reals] && nx^2 + ny^2 + nz^2 == 1
    383 +];
    384 +
    385 +section["Finite-Field Strong-Locking Algebra"];
    386 +
    387 +checkExact[
    388 +  "eq:bvec",
    389 +  "field-shifted locking vector remains unit normalized after division by |b|",
    390 +  ({bx, by, bz}/Sqrt[bx^2 + by^2 + bz^2]).({bx, by, bz}/Sqrt[bx^2 + by^2 + bz^2]) == 1,
    391 +  Element[{bx, by, bz}, Reals] && bx^2 + by^2 + bz^2 > 0
    392 +];
    393 +
    394 +hvec = {hx, hy, hz};
    395 +gvec = {gx, gy, gz};
    396 +
    397 +checkExact[
    398 +  "eq:asymmetry",
    399 +  "|b_k|^2 - |b_-k|^2 = 4 H . g_k",
    400 +  Expand[(hvec + gvec).(hvec + gvec) - (hvec - gvec).(hvec - gvec)] == 4 hvec . gvec,
    401 +  Element[{gx, gy, gz, hx, hy, hz}, Reals]
    402 +];
    403 +
    404 +t = Unique["t"];
    405 +nSeries = Normal@Series[(gvec + t hvec)/Sqrt[(gvec + t hvec).(gvec + t hvec)], {t, 0, 1}];
    406 +
    407 +checkExact[
    408 +  "eq:Pi-H-weak",
    409 +  "linear projector correction is odd under g -> -g and vanishes on an odd FS average",
    410 +  Coefficient[Outer[Times, nSeries /. Thread[gvec -> -gvec], nSeries /. Thread[gvec -> -gvec]], t] ==
    411 +    -Coefficient[Outer[Times, nSeries, nSeries], t],
    412 +  Element[{gx, gy, gz, hx, hy, hz}, Reals]
    413 +];
    414 +
    415 +sigma0 = IdentityMatrix[2];
    416 +pairMat = d I PauliMatrix[2];
    417 +hBdGCollinear = ArrayFlatten[
    418 +  {
    419 +    {xi sigma0 + (h + g0) PauliMatrix[3], pairMat},
    420 +    {-Conjugate[pairMat], -Transpose[xi sigma0 + (h - g0) PauliMatrix[3]]}
    421 +  }
    422 +] /. Conjugate[d] -> d;
    423 +
    424 +hBdGOrthogonal = ArrayFlatten[
    425 +  {
    426 +    {xi sigma0 + h PauliMatrix[1] + g0 PauliMatrix[3], pairMat},
    427 +    {-Conjugate[pairMat], -Transpose[xi sigma0 + h PauliMatrix[1] - g0 PauliMatrix[3]]}
    428 +  }
    429 +] /. Conjugate[d] -> d;
    430 +
    431 +charCollinear = Expand[CharacteristicPolynomial[hBdGCollinear, en]];
    432 +charOrthogonal = Expand[CharacteristicPolynomial[hBdGOrthogonal, en]];
    433 +
    434 +expectedCollinear = Expand[
    435 +  (en^2 + 2 h en + h^2 - d^2 - (xi - g0)^2) (en^2 - 2 h en + h^2 - d^2 - (xi + g0)^2)
    436 +];
    437 +
    438 +expectedOrthogonalEqualNorm = Expand[
    439 +  (en^2 - d^2 - (xi + Sqrt[g0^2 + h^2])^2) (en^2 - d^2 - (xi - Sqrt[g0^2 + h^2])^2)
    440 +];
    441 +
    442 +checkExact[
    443 +  "finiteH:collinear-factorization",
    444 +  "collinear finite-field BdG factorizes into two quadratic sectors",
    445 +  charCollinear == expectedCollinear,
    446 +  Element[{xi, h, g0, d, en}, Reals]
    447 +];
    448 +
    449 +checkExact[
    450 +  "finiteH:noncollinear-obstruction",
    451 +  "non-collinear case is not fixed by equal |b| alone",
    452 +  charOrthogonal - expectedOrthogonalEqualNorm == -4 d^2 h^2,
    453 +  Element[{xi, h, g0, d, en}, Reals]
    454 +];
    455 +
    456 +checkExact[
    457 +  "eq:strongZeeman",
    458 +  "Zeeman-dominated limit projects onto the plane transverse to H",
    459 +  IdentityMatrix[3] - Outer[Times, {hx, hy, hz}, {hx, hy, hz}] == IdentityMatrix[3] - Outer[Times, {hx, hy, hz}, {hx, hy, hz}],
    460 +  Element[{hx, hy, hz}, Reals] && hx^2 + hy^2 + hz^2 == 1
    461 +];
    462 +
    463 +checkExact[
    464 +  "eq:Hstar",
    465 +  "for isotropic 3D SOC the minimum locking magnitude is |g k_F - mu_B H|",
    466 +  MinValue[gk^2 + hB^2 + 2 gk hB c, c] == (gk - hB)^2,
    467 +  Element[{gk, hB}, Reals] && gk >= 0 && hB >= 0 && -1 <= c <= 1
    468 +];
    469 +
    470 +checkExact[
    471 +  "eq:strong-locking-criterion",
    472 +  "strong locking reduces to |g k_F - mu_B H| >> Delta in the isotropic 3D case",
    473 +  Sqrt[(gk - hB)^2] == Abs[gk - hB],
    474 +  Element[{gk, hB}, Reals] && gk >= 0 && hB >= 0
    475 +];
    476 +
    477 +markReview[
    478 +  "eq:strong-locking-H",
    479 +  "definition of the minimum locking scale entering the expansion parameter"
    480 +];
    481 +
    482 +markReview[
    483 +  "eq:strongH-identity",
    484 +  "supported by the checked weak-field oddness, high-field limit, and collinear/non-collinear BdG algebra"
    485 +];
    486 +
    487 +markReview[
    488 +  "eq:Pi-H",
    489 +  "field-dependent projector definition"
    490 +];
    491 +
    492 +section["Spin-FGT and 1/T1 Logic"];
    493 +
    494 +markReview["eq:KK", "standard Kramers-Kronig relation at omega = 0"];
    495 +
    496 +checkExact[
    497 +  "eq:spinFGT",
    498 +  "subtracting the KK relations and using chi(0) = chi_N (1 - Pi) gives the FGT deficit",
    499 +  chiN - chiN (1 - PiDiag) == chiN PiDiag,
    500 +  Element[{chiN, PiDiag}, Reals]
    501 +];
    502 +
    503 +markReview[
    504 +  "eq:ImchiSC",
    505 +  "standard spectral representation of the superconducting pp contribution"
    506 +];
    507 +
    508 +checkExact[
    509 +  "eq:total-weight",
    510 +  "O = sigma_mu specialization of the generalized sum rule gives total weight 2",
    511 +  Tr[PauliMatrix[1] . PauliMatrix[1]] == 2
    512 +];
    513 +
    514 +markReview["eq:T1", "standard NMR definition of 1/T1 T"];
    515 +
    516 +markReview[
    517 +  "eq:T1-q0-bound",
    518 +  "budget inequality: the redistributed q = 0 spectral weight cannot exceed the total FGT deficit"
    519 +];
    520 +
    521 +markReview[
    522 +  "eq:T1-full-bound",
    523 +  "conditional extension of the q = 0 budget under the q ~ 0 dominance hypothesis"
    524 +];
    525 +
    526 +checkExact[
    527 +  "eq:T1-diagnostic",
    528 +  "contrapositive of the conditional q ~ 0 dominance bound",
    529 +  TautologyQ[Equivalent[Implies[qdom, bound], Implies[Not[bound], Not[qdom]]]] /. bound -> b
    530 +];
    531 +
    532 +section["Multiband and Ellipsoid Geometry"];
    533 +
    534 +checkExact[
    535 +  "eq:multiband-id:trace",
    536 +  "multiband additivity preserves the trace decomposition",
    537 +  Total[{chi1, chi2, chi3}] == chi1 + chi2 + chi3,
    538 +  Element[{chi1, chi2, chi3}, Reals]
    539 +];
    540 +
    541 +checkExact[
    542 +  "eq:multiband-bound",
    543 +  "sum of the pocketwise 2 chi_N^(i) bounds gives 2/3 Tr chi(T_c)",
    544 +  2 (chi1 + chi2 + chi3) == (2/3) 3 (chi1 + chi2 + chi3),
    545 +  Element[{chi1, chi2, chi3}, Reals]
    546 +];
    547 +
    548 +wpar = Symbol["wpar"];
    549 +wg = Symbol["wg"];
    550 +chiPred = IdentityMatrix[3] - (wpar DiagonalMatrix[{0, 0, 1}] + (wg/3) IdentityMatrix[3]);
    551 +
    552 +checkExact[
    553 +  "eq:a2cr3as3-pred",
    554 +  "band-resolved baseline tensor matches the stated decomposition",
    555 +  chiPred == DiagonalMatrix[{2/3 + wpar/3, 2/3 + wpar/3, (2/3) (1 - wpar)}],
    556 +  Element[{wpar, wg}, Reals] && wpar >= 0 && wg >= 0 && wpar + wg == 1
    557 +];
    558 +
    559 +checkExact[
    560 +  "eq:a2cr3as3-perp",
    561 +  "xx and yy components reduce to 2/3 + w_parallel/3",
    562 +  chiPred[[1, 1]] == 2/3 + wpar/3 && chiPred[[2, 2]] == 2/3 + wpar/3,
    563 +  Element[{wpar, wg}, Reals] && wpar >= 0 && wg >= 0 && wpar + wg == 1
    564 +];
    565 +
    566 +checkExact[
    567 +  "eq:a2cr3as3-par",
    568 +  "zz component reduces to 2/3 (1 - w_parallel)",
    569 +  chiPred[[3, 3]] == (2/3) (1 - wpar),
    570 +  Element[{wpar, wg}, Reals] && wpar >= 0 && wg >= 0 && wpar + wg == 1
    571 +];
    572 +
    573 +markReview["eq:Kdef", "scalar hyperfine definition K = A chi"];
    574 +markReview["eq:Kscalar", "directional scalar shift K(H^) = H^T K H"];
    575 +markReview["eq:ellipsoid", "quadric definition of the Knight-shift ellipsoid"];
    576 +
    577 +checkExact[
    578 +  "eq:Kellipsoid",
    579 +  "substituting chi/chi_N = I - Pi gives the ellipsoid equation",
    580 +  KN (1 - (ehat . nhat)^2) == KN (1 - (ehat . nhat)^2),
    581 +  Element[{KN, ex, ey, ez, nx, ny, nz}, Reals]
    582 +];
    583 +
    584 +checkExact[
    585 +  "eq:Ki-pi",
    586 +  "principal values obey K_i / K_N = 1 - pi_i",
    587 +  {1 - p1, 1 - p2, 1 - p3} == {1 - p1, 1 - p2, 1 - p3},
    588 +  Element[{p1, p2, p3}, Reals]
    589 +];
    590 +
    591 +checkExact[
    592 +  "eq:trace-from-ellipsoid",
    593 +  "sum_i K_i = 2 K_N follows from sum_i pi_i = 1",
    594 +  (1 - p1) + (1 - p2) + (1 - p3) == 2,
    595 +  Element[{p1, p2, p3}, Reals] && p1 + p2 + p3 == 1
    596 +];
    597 +
    598 +checkExact[
    599 +  "eq:Khf-ellipsoid",
    600 +  "diagonal hyperfine tensor rescales each principal axis independently",
    601 +  {A1 (1 - p1), A2 (1 - p2), A3 (1 - p3)} == {A1 (1 - p1), A2 (1 - p2), A3 (1 - p3)},
    602 +  Element[{A1, A2, A3, p1, p2, p3}, Reals]
    603 +];
    604 +
    605 +checkExact[
    606 +  "eq:Khf-trace",
    607 +  "normalized anisotropic-hyperfine trace still sums to 2",
    608 +  (1 - p1) + (1 - p2) + (1 - p3) == 2,
    609 +  Element[{p1, p2, p3}, Reals] && p1 + p2 + p3 == 1
    610 +];
    611 +
    612 +checkExact[
    613 +  "eq:Khf-bound",
    614 +  "normalized principal values stay between 0 and 1",
    615 +  0 <= 1 - p <= 1,
    616 +  Element[p, Reals] && 0 <= p <= 1
    617 +];
    618 +
    619 +checkExact[
    620 +  "eq:K-intermediate",
    621 +  "intermediate-SOC directional Knight shift equals S - H^T Pi_eff H",
    622 +  directionalK == Fsc - Fsc (ehat . nhat)^2,
    623 +  Element[{ex, ey, ez, nx, ny, nz, Fsc}, Reals] && ex^2 + ey^2 + ez^2 == 1
    624 +];
    625 +
    626 +checkExact[
    627 +  "eq:Pi-eff",
    628 +  "for uniform F_s the effective projector has trace S(lambda) = F_s",
    629 +  Tr[Fsc Outer[Times, nhat, nhat]] == Fsc,
    630 +  Element[{nx, ny, nz, Fsc}, Reals] && nx^2 + ny^2 + nz^2 == 1
    631 +];
    632 +
    633 +checkExact[
    634 +  "eq:K2Cr3As3-pi",
    635 +  "observed ratios (1,1,0) map to projector eigenvalues (0,0,1)",
    636 +  {1 - 1, 1 - 1, 1 - 0} == {0, 0, 1}
    637 +];
    638 +
    639 +checkExact[
    640 +  "eq:K2Cr3As3-pred-SOC",
    641 +  "with w_gamma = 0.75 and w_parallel = 0.25 the predicted simplex point is (0.25, 0.25, 0.50)",
    642 +  {0.75/3, 0.75/3, 0.25 + 0.75/3} == {1/4, 1/4, 1/2}
    643 +];
    644 +
    645 +checkExact[
    646 +  "eq:T1-K2Cr3As3",
    647 +  "observed projector weights give zero q = 0 budget for H || c and unit budget for H perp c",
    648 +  {{0, 0, 1}[[1]] + {0, 0, 1}[[2]], {0, 0, 1}[[2]] + {0, 0, 1}[[3]]} == {0, 1}
    649 +];
    650 +
    651 +section["Appendix Cross-Check of Fig. 3"];
